       <article class="post-65366 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-human-rights-2 category-jobs category-ontario-government category-subsidies-costs category-viability category-wind-industry" id="post-65366">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/07/18/the-green-job-joke-in-ontario/" rel="bookmark">
           The Green Job “Joke” in Ontario
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/07/18/the-green-job-joke-in-ontario/" rel="bookmark" title="09:32">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-07-18T09:32:17+00:00">
            07/18/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/07/18/the-green-job-joke-in-ontario/#comments">
           14
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          “Green Jobs” have always been a bit of a joke. Although not a very funny one.
         </p>
         <p>
          Back in 2010 McGuinty signed a deal with South Korean company Samsung, and promised Ontarians that all kinds of employment would flow from it.
         </p>
         <p style="padding-left: 60px;">
          The Liberal government ended months of speculation in September when it confirmed it was in talks with Samsung about a project that could create about
          <strong>
           15,000 jobs
          </strong>
          .
         </p>
         <p style="padding-left: 60px;">
          Ontario’s manufacturing sector has shed hundreds of thousands of jobs in the recession. The deal with Samsung would likely be the linchpin in McGuinty’s push for renewable sources of energy and his plan to create
          <strong>
           50,000
          </strong>
          jobs.
          <a href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/toronto/samsung-deal-to-bring-wind-solar-farms-to-ont-sources-1.887072" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
           CBC, 2010
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter wp-image-24615 size-full" data-attachment-id="24615" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;MARK BLINCH&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;Ontario Premier Dalton McGuinty (L) and CEO of Samsung C&amp;T Chi Sung Ha shake hands in Toronto January 21, 2010.  A South Korean consortium led by Samsung C&amp;T Corporation has won a $6 billion deal to supply renewable energy equipment to Canada's Ontario province, the company said on Thursday. REUTERS\/Mark Blinch (CANADA - Tags: BUSINESS POLITICS ENERGY SCI TECH)&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;1264032000&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Ontario Premier McGuinty and CEO of Samsung C&amp;T Chi shake hands in Toronto&quot;}" data-image-title="Ontario Premier McGuinty and CEO of Samsung C&amp;amp;T Chi shake hands in Toronto" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/05/e5105c5048c1993397b766cbea6e.jpg?fit=584%2C371" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/05/e5105c5048c1993397b766cbea6e.jpg?fit=300%2C190" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/05/e5105c5048c1993397b766cbea6e.jpg?fit=615%2C391" data-orig-size="615,391" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2011/05/12/book-claims-samsung-is-basically-the-most-corrupt-company-in-asia/ontario-premier-mcguinty-and-ceo-of-samsung-ct-chi-shake-hands-in-toronto/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="371" sizes="(max-width: 584px) 100vw, 584px" src="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/05/e5105c5048c1993397b766cbea6e.jpg?resize=584%2C371" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/05/e5105c5048c1993397b766cbea6e.jpg?w=615 615w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/05/e5105c5048c1993397b766cbea6e.jpg?resize=150%2C95 150w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/05/e5105c5048c1993397b766cbea6e.jpg?resize=300%2C190 300w" width="584"/>
         </p>
         <p>
          The numbers were highly inflated in that press release. Even Samsung’s website could only cough up minuscule (although inconsistent) numbers.
         </p>
         <p style="padding-left: 60px;">
          Thanks to Samsung’s Green Energy Investment Agreement with the Government of Ontario, we are creating
          <strong>
           9,000 jobs
          </strong>
          , kick-starting a new industry in Ontario and generate 1,369 megawatts of clean energy.
          <a href="http://www.samsungrenewableenergy.ca" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
           Samsung Renewable Energy
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="padding-left: 60px;">
          Samsung and Pattern Energy’s wind power projects in Ontario are creating more than
          <strong>
           1,000 jobs
          </strong>
          <a href="http://www.samsungrenewableenergy.ca/node/74" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
           Samsung Renewable Energy, 2014
          </a>
         </p>
         <p style="padding-left: 60px;">
          Our investments will create
          <strong>
           900 direct renewable energy manufacturing jobs
          </strong>
          and 9,000 high-skilled jobs in Ontario.
          <a href="http://www.samsungrenewableenergy.ca/node/74" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
           Samsung Renewable Energy, 2014
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Down down down the number fell! We went from a promised 15,000 Samsung jobs in 2010, to a possible 900 in 2014? So what is the real number? I suppose nobody is really counting anymore. The fact is the province blatantly lied to the people of Ontario just so this juicy deal could be pushed through without much fuss. One would think the opposition parities would do as much as they could to investigate WHY this deal had to be made…
          <a class="more-link" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/07/18/the-green-job-joke-in-ontario/#more-65366">
           Continue reading
           <span class="meta-nav">
            →
           </span>
          </a>
         </p>

       <!-- #post-65366 -->
       <article class="post-65306 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-ministry-of-the-environment-ontario category-noise category-ontario-government" id="post-65306">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/06/02/ministry-of-environment-did-not-investigate-over-68-of-wind-turbine-noise-complaints-received/" rel="bookmark">
           Ministry of Environment did not investigate over 68% of wind turbine noise complaints received
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/06/02/ministry-of-environment-did-not-investigate-over-68-of-wind-turbine-noise-complaints-received/" rel="bookmark" title="18:15">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-06-02T18:15:58+00:00">
            06/02/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/06/02/ministry-of-environment-did-not-investigate-over-68-of-wind-turbine-noise-complaints-received/#comments">
           39
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="437" src="http://globalnews.ca/video/embed/3498008/" width="670">
          </iframe>
         </p>
         <p>
          Brian Hill,
          <a href="http://globalnews.ca/news/3490234/ontario-wind-turbines-family-complaints/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           Global News
           <br/>
          </a>
          Excerpt: “Over the past two years, officials from the ministry have measured violations of the province’s noise limits at the couple’s home on two occasions, first in August 2015 and again in March 2017. Despite these violations, the couple says the government has done nothing other than order more tests.
         </p>
         <p>
          The Stachura’s complaints of government inaction are not unique. In fact, Global News has learned that Ontario’s Ministry of the Environment and Climate Change does not respond to the majority of complaints made by residents concerned about wind turbines.
         </p>
         <p>
          Documents released through Ontario’s Freedom of Information Act and obtained by Global News reveal officials from the Ministry of Environment chose not to investigate or deferred responding to – meaning they did not make immediate plans to investigate – roughly 68 per cent of all noise and health complaints lodged against wind turbine operators in the province between 2006 and 2014. This represents nearly 2,200 individual complaints.
         </p>
         <p>
          The documents also show limited resources sometimes prevented the ministry from responding to complaints.”
          <a href="http://globalnews.ca/news/3490234/ontario-wind-turbines-family-complaints/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <iframe frameborder="0" height="180px" src="https://omny.fm/shows/tasha-kheiriddin/what-is-the-ontario-ministry-of-environment-doing/embed?style=artwork" width="100%">
          </iframe>
         </p>
         <hr/>
         <p>
          <strong>
           <a href="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/01/wind-farm-noise-map.gif">
            <img alt="" class="alignright size-medium wp-image-19643" data-attachment-id="19643" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="wind-farm-noise-map" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/01/wind-farm-noise-map.gif?fit=300%2C393" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/01/wind-farm-noise-map.gif?fit=229%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/01/wind-farm-noise-map.gif?fit=300%2C393" data-orig-size="300,393" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2011/01/09/health-effects-of-turbines-we-already-know/wind-farm-noise-map/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="300" sizes="(max-width: 229px) 100vw, 229px" src="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/01/wind-farm-noise-map.gif?resize=229%2C300" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/01/wind-farm-noise-map.gif?resize=229%2C300 229w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2011/01/wind-farm-noise-map.gif?resize=114%2C150 114w" width="229"/>
           </a>
           Unaddressed Wind Turbine Complaints Anger Local Group
          </strong>
          <br/>
          <span class="post-byline">
           by Miranda Chant,
           <a href="http://blackburnnews.com/london/london-news/2017/05/31/unaddressed-wind-turbine-complaints-anger-local-group/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Blackburn News
           </a>
           <br/>
          </span>
          A local group opposed to wind turbines is once again calling on the province to put a stop to the controversial wind power projects, after a new report found many noise complaints related to the turbines are being ignored.
         </p>
         <p>
          Dutton Dunwich Opponents of Wind Turbines (DDOWT), a group made up people from the rural community southwest of London, has written to Ontario Minister of the Environment and Climate Change (MOECC) Glenn Murray demanding he stop any new wind turbine approvals.
         </p>
         <p>
          Their demand comes in light of documents obtained by Wind Concerns Ontario under the Freedom of Information Act. The documents show the Ministry of Environment chose not to investigate or deferred responding to roughly 68% of all noise and health complaints made against green energy operators in the province between 2006 and 2014.
         </p>
         <p>
          A list of 3,180 complaints is included in the documents. Of those, more than 1,700 were not investigated by the ministry. In another 446 of the complaints the ministry deferred responding. Complainants reported sleep disturbances, headaches, and dizziness from the wind turbine noise emissions.
          <a href="http://blackburnnews.com/london/london-news/2017/05/31/unaddressed-wind-turbine-complaints-anger-local-group/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>
         <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
          <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon sd-sharing">

       <article class="post-65294 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-ethics category-ontario-government category-subsidies-costs category-viability category-wind-industry" id="post-65294">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/28/ontario-govt-ignored-chance-to-cut-1-5b-in-hydro-bills-documents/" rel="bookmark">
           Ontario gov’t ignored chance to cut $1.5B in hydro bills: documents
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/28/ontario-govt-ignored-chance-to-cut-1-5b-in-hydro-bills-documents/" rel="bookmark" title="07:08">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-05-28T07:08:02+00:00">
            05/28/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/28/ontario-govt-ignored-chance-to-cut-1-5b-in-hydro-bills-documents/#comments">
           7
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="270" scrolling="no" src="https://bmplayer-a.akamaihd.net/shareable/embedssl.html?dc=ctvnews_web&amp;cid=875183&amp;col=379&amp;w=480&amp;h=270&amp;pl=0&amp;plh=0&amp;adSite=ctv.ctvnews&amp;adZone=home&amp;omniAcct=ctvgmnews,ctvgmnewsglobalsuite&amp;section=CTVNews&amp;site=ctvnews&amp;shareUrl=http://www.ctvnews.ca/video?clipId=875183&amp;v7=canada&amp;v8=story&amp;v9=&amp;v10=" width="480">
          </iframe>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="size-medium wp-image-48843 alignright" data-attachment-id="48843" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="wind scam inquiry" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047.jpg?fit=584%2C438" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047.jpg?fit=300%2C225" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047.jpg?fit=1024%2C768" data-orig-size="1024,768" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2012/11/02/pics-of-good-riddance-protest-on-mcguinty-in-london-today/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="225" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047.jpg?resize=300%2C225" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047.jpg?resize=300%2C225 300w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047.jpg?resize=150%2C112 150w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/2012-keiths-birthday-protest-dalton-047.jpg?w=1024 1024w" width="300"/>
          </a>
          <a href="http://www.ctvnews.ca/canada/ontario-gov-t-ignored-chance-to-cut-1-5b-in-hydro-bills-documents-1.2912611#" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           CTV News
          </a>
          <br/>
          Newly unearthed documents suggest Ontario’s Liberal government could have saved hydro customers $1.5 billion by terminating an agreement with Samsung, but decided against it.
         </p>
         <p>
          The papers, uncovered by Progressive Conservative Finance Critic Vic Fedeli, relate to the 2009 Samsung green energy agreement that would take $10.5 billion from Ontario hydro bills, and pay it to a Samsung consortium over 20 years. In return, Samsung would deliver green energy and build factories in the province, employing 900 people.
         </p>
         <p>
          Four years into the deal, however, a confidential document from staff at the Ministry of Energy advised the government it could save hydro customers $5.2 billion by terminating the agreement. This was because the Korean consortium was missing contract targets and deadlines on electricity projects that Ontario didn’t even need anymore.
         </p>
         <p>
          But instead of calling off the deal, the Liberals renegotiated the contract to save only $3.7 billion –leaving $1.5 billion in hydro savings on the table.
         </p>
         <p>
          “Even though we don’t need the power, and even though we can get out of this for nothing, (the Liberals) already told the public how important this deal is,” Fedeli told CTV Toronto, suggesting that the government ignored the potential savings “just to save face.”
          <a href="http://www.ctvnews.ca/canada/ontario-gov-t-ignored-chance-to-cut-1-5b-in-hydro-bills-documents-1.2912611#" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>

       <!-- #post-65294 -->
       <article class="post-65286 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-bats-and-birds category-environmental" id="post-65286">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/26/wind-developers-deploy-ultrasonic-units-to-jam-bat-echolocation/" rel="bookmark">
           Wind developers deploy ultrasonic units to ‘jam’ bat echolocation
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/26/wind-developers-deploy-ultrasonic-units-to-jam-bat-echolocation/" rel="bookmark" title="17:20">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-05-26T17:20:12+00:00">
            05/26/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/26/wind-developers-deploy-ultrasonic-units-to-jam-bat-echolocation/#comments">
           15
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="size-medium wp-image-62382 alignright" data-attachment-id="62382" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"5.6","credit":"","camera":"Canon EOS DIGITAL REBEL XT","caption":"UNDATED -  Erin Baerwalk examining a dead Hoary bat on Wild Energy Facilities near Pincher Creek, Alberta in August 2006.  Handout Photo: Monty Nicol    For Margaret Munro (Canwest) Story","created_timestamp":"1154320063","copyright":"","focal_length":"76","iso":"100","shutter_speed":"0.0025","title":"CNSPhoto-Munro-Bats","orientation":"1"}' data-image-title="CNSPhoto-Munro-Bats" data-large-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?fit=584%2C389" data-medium-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?fit=300%2C199" data-orig-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?fit=620%2C413" data-orig-size="620,413" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2014/11/19/wind-turbines-causing-thousands-of-bats-to-die-of-collapsed-lungs-annually-in-alberta-top-bat-expert/cnsphoto-munro-bats/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="199" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?resize=300%2C199" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?resize=300%2C199 300w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?resize=150%2C99 150w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?w=620 620w" width="300"/>
          </a>
          NextEra
          <a href="http://www.nexteraenergycanada.com/pdf/jericho/Project%20Modifications%202017/WJC%20-%20complete%20package.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           is sticking Ultrasonic Units on their Jericho, Goshen and Bluewater wind turbines
          </a>
          for the purpose of deterring bats from flying near them.
         </p>
         <p>
          Perhaps this wouldn’t piss me off so much if pre-construction they had absolutely no idea that bats were going to be killed by their machines.
         </p>
         <p>
          But they did. And they built them anyways. Now what is their solution?
         </p>
         <p>
          To “jam” (their word) the bat’s echolocation with ultrasonic frequencies. Then they won’t be able to communicate or know where the fuck (yeah I’m mad) they are flying, and will h
          <span class="text_exposed_show">
           opefully flee to some non-turbine infested area, if they still exist anywhere locally. I believe this is called “habitat displacement”, which
           <a href="https://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2011/06/03/dr-scott-petrie-potential-impact-of-wind-turbine-development-on-waterfowl/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Dr. Scott Petrie warned all the wind developers
           </a>
           of over and over for the past half dozen years.
          </span>
         </p>
         <div class="text_exposed_show">
          <p>
           Ah, but NextEra and their ilk are “good green corporate citizens” – they wouldn’t take part in something so repulsive as this, would they? They did it to humans so maybe…
          </p>
          <p>
           The problem for the wind company is not the laborious and tedious job of picking up all the dead bat carcasses (a bloody pain I suspect though), it’s the horrid “mitigation” that they are forced to do when they exceed the “kill threshold” of birds, bats and raptors set by the Ministry of Natural Resources – they are exceeding them all the freakin’ time!
          </p>
          <p>
           Supposedly the MNR will sometimes make the wind companies that exceed their kill limits, “curtail” (shut down) their turbines during peak migration, night or in low winds when the bats are out and about. (Honestly I highly doubt anyone is watching or monitoring, but lets give them the benefit of the doubt here). That lost production really sucks for the wind companies ’cause they are loosing way too much $$. Every little penny counts for their greedy little hearts.
          </p>
          <p>
           Again, the problem is not the killing of Endangered Species (which is what is happening, with impunity), that doesn’t bother the wind company at all or they would shut their turbines down most willingly.
          </p>
          <p>
           Instead they employ these fancy new Ultrasonic blasters to scare those little buggers away. Because that’s what good neighbours do when they come to a land full of Endangered Species. They wreck their homes. You know, like
           <a href="http://www.simcoereformer.ca/2013/01/07/outrage-in-haldimand-over-bald-eagle-nest-removal" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            eagle nests
           </a>
           and stuff.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a href="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg">
            <img alt="" class="alignleft size-large wp-image-65287" data-attachment-id="65287" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"1"}' data-image-title="bat deterrent" data-large-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?fit=584%2C222" data-medium-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?fit=300%2C114" data-orig-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?fit=1161%2C441" data-orig-size="1161,441" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/26/wind-developers-deploy-ultrasonic-units-to-jam-bat-echolocation/bat-deterrent/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="222" sizes="(max-width: 584px) 100vw, 584px" src="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?resize=584%2C222" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?resize=1024%2C389 1024w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?resize=150%2C57 150w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?resize=300%2C114 300w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?resize=768%2C292 768w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?resize=500%2C190 500w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/bat-deterrent.jpg?w=1161 1161w" width="584"/>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p>
           Here’s
           <a href="http://www.nexteraenergycanada.com/pdf/jericho/Project%20Modifications%202017/WJC%20-%20complete%20package.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            their sales pitch
           </a>
           :
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            “Instead of curtailing to avoid take, deter bats from the turbine”
           </strong>
           <br/>
           <em>
            (“Take”, for those unfamiliar with the lingo, is “kill”. Sounds nicer, eh? Note also this is all about avoiding curtailment, not avoiding bat kill, and certainly not avoiding destruction of habitat!)
           </em>
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            “Many bats rely on echolocation for orienting, foraging and communication – Echolocation “jamming” most effective defense against bats ever documented.”
           </strong>
           <em>
            (So they recognize what the bats needs to survive, and then wallop them with a baseball bat. Note also they use the negative wording, “defence
            <strong>
             against
            </strong>
            bats”. That shows their true colours on this issue.)
           </em>
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            “Deterrent units create a broad range of frequencies to deter different bat species”
           </strong>
           <br/>
           (
           <em>
            Oh well, wind developers know all about ‘broad ranges of frequencies’ to deter human beings, so I believe them!)
           </em>
          </p>
          <p>
           Here’s another thought. How is a wind developer, or anyone for that matter, permitted to disrupt an Endangered Species habitat like this? What exactly is the purpose of the supposed protection of the Act if wind developers are allowed to kill, harm, harass and maim them as much as they want?! Aren’t developers usually penalized for this kind of deliberate destruction?
          </p>
          <p>
           ~ Esther
          </p>
         </div>

       <article class="post-65271 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-health category-ministry-of-health category-ontario-government" id="post-65271">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/16/medical-officer-of-health-does-not-have-the-authority-to-stop-noxious-wind-turbines/" rel="bookmark">
           Medical Officer of Health does not have the authority to stop noxious wind turbines
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/16/medical-officer-of-health-does-not-have-the-authority-to-stop-noxious-wind-turbines/" rel="bookmark" title="09:36">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-05-16T09:36:33+00:00">
            05/16/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/05/16/medical-officer-of-health-does-not-have-the-authority-to-stop-noxious-wind-turbines/#comments">
           21
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/1006250026.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignright wp-image-62204 size-medium" data-attachment-id="62204" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"5.6","credit":"","camera":"FinePix S1500","caption":"","created_timestamp":"1277460570","copyright":"","focal_length":"12.6","iso":"64","shutter_speed":"0.00222222222222","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="health hazard" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/1006250026.jpg?fit=584%2C787" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/1006250026.jpg?fit=222%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/1006250026.jpg?fit=760%2C1024" data-orig-size="760,1024" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2014/10/16/wind-development-a-hazard-to-human-health-declares-brown-county-board-of-health/attachment/1006250026/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="300" sizes="(max-width: 222px) 100vw, 222px" src="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/1006250026.jpg?resize=222%2C300" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/1006250026.jpg?resize=222%2C300 222w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/1006250026.jpg?resize=111%2C150 111w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/1006250026.jpg?w=760 760w" width="222"/>
          </a>
          Just in case we thought the wind turbines would be ordered to be mitigated or shut down  if health problems were noticed in the Huron County Health study – nope that’s not gonna happen. Read the correspondence below and you will realize that it is all just ‘process’, with no action to ‘correct’ on the horizon. Basically more people are just being used as test subjects. That’s it. And that’s flat out unacceptable.
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Thanks to
           <a href="https://cs.uwaterloo.ca/~mannr/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Richard Mann
           </a>
           , Associate Professor  Department of Computer Science; University of Waterloo for this.
          </em>
         </p>
         <hr/>
         <p>
          From: Erica Clark
          <br/>
          Sent: Friday, May 12, 2017 3:44 PM
          <br/>
          Subject: Ability of MOH to write orders against wind turbines under section 13 of HPPA
         </p>
         <p>
          Hello,
         </p>
         <p>
          One of the issues the University of Waterloo ethics committee asked us to address was the hope residents had that, at some time, the Medical Officer of Health would be able to write an order curtailing or shutting down the wind turbines. We had already stated in the recruitment materials that the study would not generate sufficient evidence to prove wind turbines cause health problems (establishing causality) but the ethics committee questioned whether we were providing enough information on the limits of the Medical Officer of Health’s authority. To address that concern, we have spoken with individuals experienced in interpreting the Health Protection and Promotion Act (HPPA) specifically, sections 11 (investigating health hazards) and 13 (writing orders). They provided us with the attached documents that outline the limits on the MOH’s authority to write orders.
         </p>
         <p>
          The first document (Pelletier v Northwestern Health Unit) is the proceedings from an Ontario Health Services Appeal and Review Board and the second (Court File 2006-01-04) is a judicial review of the appeal hearing by the Ontario Superior Court of Justice. Essentially, these documents state that when the Legislature places the authority to regulate with one organization, such as municipal councils or the Ministry of the Environment, the courts do not accept that there was an intention to give the same authority to the MOH under section 13 of the HPPA. The rulings were made when the Northwestern Health Unit MOH wrote orders prohibiting exposure to environmental tobacco smoke (second hand smoke) in several bars and restaurants. At the time the orders were written, exposure to environmental tobacco smoke was (and still is) deemed a health hazard.
         </p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>
           Since the Legislature assigned the duty to regulate wind turbines to the Ministry of the Environment and not the health units, the courts will not recognize the authority of the MOH under section 13 of the HPPA to write an order curtailing or shutting down the wind turbines.
          </p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>
          I will be putting these documents on the health unit website soon, however, I wanted you to have a chance to read them first. The documents are publicly available at
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           <a href="https://l.facebook.com/l.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.canlii.org%2Fen%2Fon%2Fonhsarb%2Fdoc%2F2004%2F2004canlii69635%2F2004canlii69635.html&amp;h=ATMEFbHrWIHZZmrSNDUnn9XwROmyv2QaP4HcFSC6ExsKxaCi5wWsXxKvRQ4DtJAMISm-FosMA-uFyUAljbNzLfXSFb2sCeI3PKDppE-6Z3MktumtTmLXWRYYAzax9vjT33yGY-1u0XzFo4sE4Q" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            www.canlii.org/en/on/onhsarb/doc/2004/2004canlii69635/2004canlii69635.html
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           <a href="https://l.facebook.com/l.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.canlii.org%2Fen%2Fon%2Fonhsarb%2Fdoc%2F2004%2F2004canlii69635%2F2004canlii69635.html&amp;h=ATMEFbHrWIHZZmrSNDUnn9XwROmyv2QaP4HcFSC6ExsKxaCi5wWsXxKvRQ4DtJAMISm-FosMA-uFyUAljbNzLfXSFb2sCeI3PKDppE-6Z3MktumtTmLXWRYYAzax9vjT33yGY-1u0XzFo4sE4Q" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            www.canlii.org/en/on/onhsarb/doc/2004/2004canlii69635/2004canlii69635.html
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           <a href="https://l.facebook.com/l.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.canlii.org%2Fen%2Fon%2Fonhsarb%2Fdoc%2F2004%2F2004canlii69635%2F2004canlii69635.html&amp;h=ATMEFbHrWIHZZmrSNDUnn9XwROmyv2QaP4HcFSC6ExsKxaCi5wWsXxKvRQ4DtJAMISm-FosMA-uFyUAljbNzLfXSFb2sCeI3PKDppE-6Z3MktumtTmLXWRYYAzax9vjT33yGY-1u0XzFo4sE4Q" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            www.canlii.org/en/on/onhsarb/doc/2004/2004canlii69635/2004canlii69635.html
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           And
           <a href="https://l.facebook.com/l.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.ontariocourts.ca%2Fsearch-canlii%2Fscj%2Fdv-en.htm&amp;h=ATMEFbHrWIHZZmrSNDUnn9XwROmyv2QaP4HcFSC6ExsKxaCi5wWsXxKvRQ4DtJAMISm-FosMA-uFyUAljbNzLfXSFb2sCeI3PKDppE-6Z3MktumtTmLXWRYYAzax9vjT33yGY-1u0XzFo4sE4Q" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            www.ontariocourts.ca/search-canlii/scj/dv-en.htm
           </a>
           .
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p>
          Thanks
         </p>
         <p>
          Erica
         </p>
         <p>
          ____________________________________
          <br/>
          Erica Clark, PhD
          <br/>
          Epidemiologist, APHEO Secretary
          <br/>
          Huron County Health Unit
          <br/>
          77722B London Rd., RR #5
          <br/>
          Clinton, ON N0M 1L0
          <br/>
          519.482.3416 ext. 2022
          <br/>
          Toll-free 1.877.837.6143
          <br/>
          www.huronhealthunit.ca
          <br/>
          eclark@huroncounty.ca
         </p>

       <!-- #post-65271 -->
       <article class="post-65179 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-ontario-government" id="post-65179">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/30/wind-still-fills-sails-of-wynne-arrogance/" rel="bookmark">
           Wind still fills sails of Wynne arrogance
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/30/wind-still-fills-sails-of-wynne-arrogance/" rel="bookmark" title="08:38">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-03-30T08:38:47+00:00">
            03/30/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/30/wind-still-fills-sails-of-wynne-arrogance/#comments">
           24
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.lfpress.com/2017/03/29/wind-still-fills-sails-of-wynne-arrogance" target="_blank">
           London Free Press
           <br/>
          </a>
          Only in Kathleen Wynne’s Ontario would we still be spending money we don’t have, to build wind farms few people want, to generate electricity we don’t need.
         </p>
         <p>
          And yet that’s exactly what’s happening six months after the government halted its green energy policy. Planning for five new wind turbine developments continues despite admission from the Wynne government that Ontario won’t use the electricity these turbines will generate.
         </p>
         <p>
          Indeed, if history is any indication, the excess electricity generated from turbines yet to be built will be sold at a steep
          <a href="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/wynne-not-a-willing-host.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignleft size-medium wp-image-58898" data-attachment-id="58898" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="wynne not a willing host" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/wynne-not-a-willing-host.jpg?fit=584%2C779" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/wynne-not-a-willing-host.jpg?fit=225%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/wynne-not-a-willing-host.jpg?fit=600%2C800" data-orig-size="600,800" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2013/11/12/wind-turbines-remain-a-turbulent-issue-in-perth-wellington/wynne-not-a-willing-host/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="300" sizes="(max-width: 225px) 100vw, 225px" src="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/wynne-not-a-willing-host.jpg?resize=225%2C300" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/wynne-not-a-willing-host.jpg?resize=225%2C300 225w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/wynne-not-a-willing-host.jpg?resize=112%2C150 112w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/wynne-not-a-willing-host.jpg?w=600 600w" width="225"/>
          </a>
          discount, probably to American states that already offer electricity cheaper than Ontario’s, states that in some cases are using cheap electricity to lure away Ontario business.
         </p>
         <p>
          The Ontario government says it’s contractually obligated to allow the last of these wind turbine developers to bring their plans to fruition. A sensible response would be to cancel the contracts and pay whatever legal penalties might follow. But no, the Wynne government will stoically follow through.
          <a href="http://www.lfpress.com/2017/03/29/wind-still-fills-sails-of-wynne-arrogance" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>

          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/category/setbacks/" rel="category tag">
           Setbacks
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="sep">

         </span>

       <article class="post-65132 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-ontario-government" id="post-65132">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/05/wind-turbines-a-government-backed-ponzi-scheme/" rel="bookmark">
           Wind turbines a government-backed Ponzi scheme
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/05/wind-turbines-a-government-backed-ponzi-scheme/" rel="bookmark" title="19:12">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-03-05T19:12:57+00:00">
            03/05/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/05/wind-turbines-a-government-backed-ponzi-scheme/#comments">
           28
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/fat-cat-wind-scam.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignright size-full wp-image-49019" data-attachment-id="49019" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="fat cat wind scam" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/fat-cat-wind-scam.jpg?fit=211%2C239" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/fat-cat-wind-scam.jpg?fit=211%2C239" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/fat-cat-wind-scam.jpg?fit=211%2C239" data-orig-size="211,239" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2012/11/09/wind-things-are-not-green/fat-cat-wind-scam/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="239" sizes="(max-width: 211px) 100vw, 211px" src="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/fat-cat-wind-scam.jpg?resize=211%2C239" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/fat-cat-wind-scam.jpg?w=211 211w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/fat-cat-wind-scam.jpg?resize=132%2C150 132w" width="211"/>
          </a>
          <a href="http://www.nugget.ca/2017/03/05/wind-turbines-a-government-backed-ponzi-scheme" target="_blank">
           North Bay Nugget
          </a>
          <br/>
          All you people out there complaining about your hydro prices need to realize some important facts about the Kathleen Wynne government.
         </p>
         <ol>
          <li>
           The global adjustment charge on your hydro bill is to pay for the giant industrial wind turbines Wynne  has placed all  over rural Ontario.
          </li>
          <li>
           Wind turbines a useless technology that destroys our rural environment, ruins people’s health and poisons our drinking water aquifers.
          </li>
          <li>
           The only reason these turbines were erected was so Liberal insiders and their friends could get filthy rich.
          </li>
          <li>
           Wynne will not cancel the turbine projects or reduce the subsidies because the turbine lobbyists know where the political bodies are buried.
          </li>
          <li>
           Wynne has taken away the democratic rights of the people for her own financial and political gain.
          </li>
          <li>
           Wynne has sacrificed the health of rural citizens just so her friends can get rich.
          </li>
          <li>
           In a few year’s time, when it inevitably collapses, this wind turbine scam will be revealed for what it is: An enormous government-backed Ponzi scheme, founded on greed, corruption and stupidity.
          </li>
         </ol>
         <p>
          Leonard Vandenbosch
          <br/>
          West Grey, Ont
         </p>

        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          Have a good look at these recent and disturbing pictures posted on

         <hr/>
         <p>
          Flashback much?
         </p>
         <p>
          Who does one go to when you see wind turbines installed this close to an active nest? You know it’s just a matter of time before t
          <img class="alignright wp-image-13184 size-medium" data-attachment-id="13184" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="w-t_eagle_collision03" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/07/w-t_eagle_collision031.jpg?fit=250%2C333" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/07/w-t_eagle_collision031.jpg?fit=225%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/07/w-t_eagle_collision031.jpg?fit=250%2C333" data-orig-size="250,333" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2010/07/03/wind-power-would-sow-avian-megadeath/w-t_eagle_collision03-2/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="300" sizes="(max-width: 225px) 100vw, 225px" src="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/07/w-t_eagle_collision031.jpg?resize=225%2C300" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/07/w-t_eagle_collision031.jpg?resize=225%2C300 225w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/07/w-t_eagle_collision031.jpg?resize=112%2C150 112w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/07/w-t_eagle_collision031.jpg?w=250 250w" width="225"/>
          he residents of that nest get added to this list of carcasses found in Ontario under wind turbines:
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           X
          </strong>
          <a href="https://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2010/04/06/bald-eagle-killed-by-wind-turbine-in-norfolk-county-ontario/" target="_blank">
           2009
          </a>
          , Norfolk Wind Project – Bald Eagle
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/07/w-t_eagle_collision031.jpg">
           <br/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           X
          </strong>
          <a href="https://t.co/dANEDjQFxP" target="_blank">
           2012
          </a>
          , Talbot Wind Project –Bald Eagle
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           X
          </strong>
          <a href="https://t.co/IE8UIHlqLA" target="_blank">
           2013
          </a>
          , Talbot Wind Project – Bald Eagl
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           X
          </strong>
          <a href="https://t.co/X53S3kRFvL" target="_blank">
           2014
          </a>
          , Port Dover Wind Project – Bald Eagle
         </p>
         <p>
          You want to help. The government makes all the rules and regulations for what any person/developer can do around important habitat like this, so they are the first you think of. Except… that they have a really bad track record on this.
         </p>
         <p>
          <img alt="" class="alignright wp-image-54858" data-attachment-id="54858" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"5.6","credit":"","camera":"DSC-HX100V","caption":"","created_timestamp":"1357387235","copyright":"","focal_length":"144","iso":"100","shutter_speed":"0.0008","title":""}' data-image-title="eagle nest" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/eagle-nest.jpg?fit=584%2C438" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/eagle-nest.jpg?fit=300%2C224" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/eagle-nest.jpg?fit=1014%2C760" data-orig-size="1014,760" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2013/05/16/windpower-no-matter-what-even-if-it-means-killing-eagle-habitat/eagle-nest-2/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="200" sizes="(max-width: 264px) 100vw, 264px" src="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/eagle-nest.jpg?resize=264%2C200" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/eagle-nest.jpg?zoom=2&amp;resize=264%2C200 528w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/eagle-nest.jpg?zoom=3&amp;resize=264%2C200 792w" width="264"/>
          Okay, lets say you go to the Ministry of Natural Resources and Forestry (MNRF), as some good citizens did in November 2012. I’ll take you back there.
         </p>
         <p>
          Warning, this is a long one, there is no other way to write it, so grab a drink.
         </p>
         <hr/>
         <p>
          <em>
           ***Last year I filed an Freedom of Information request with the MNRF for all correspondence relating to the Haldimand eagle nest destruction by NextEra Energy. I wanted to see what the hell was happening in their heads, and head offices. You can see all the files received from the FOI on this Google Drive:
          </em>
          <a href="https://drive.google.com/open?id=0B24A4SH_cewXYThGR0xjVFZpTUk" target="_blank">
           Bald Eagle Nest Destruction NextEra MNRF
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Somewhere around November 19th, 2012 the MNRF had it’s first glimpse at an issue they hadn’t dealt with before. Letters from residents in rural Haldimand County had landed on their desk – they were asking that the MNRF intervene with Florida based wind turbine developer NextEra’s construction around an active Bald Eagle nest.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/eagles.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignright size-full wp-image-49354" data-attachment-id="49354" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="eagles" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/eagles.jpg?fit=584%2C390" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/eagles.jpg?fit=300%2C200" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/eagles.jpg?fit=640%2C427" data-orig-size="640,427" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2012/11/27/nextera-turbine-within-100m-of-active-bald-eagle-nest-in-haldimand-county/eagles/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="390" sizes="(max-width: 584px) 100vw, 584px" src="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/eagles.jpg?resize=584%2C390" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/eagles.jpg?w=640 640w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/eagles.jpg?resize=150%2C100 150w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/eagles.jpg?resize=300%2C200 300w" width="584"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          The MNR wasn’t quite sure what to do.
          <a href="https://www.ontario.ca/laws/regulation/980666" target="_blank">
           The Fish and Wildlife Conservation Act
          </a>
          said:
         </p>
         <p style="padding-left: 30px;">
          <a href="http://www.ontario.ca/fr/lois/loi/97f41#s7s1">
           7.  (1)
          </a>
          A person shall not destroy, take or possess the nest or eggs of a bird that belongs to a species that is wild by nature.  1997, c. 41, s. 7 (1).
         </p>
         <p>
          But there were also exemptions made for “special” people/corporations in need of favours:
         </p>
         <p style="padding-left: 30px;">
          <a href="http://www.ontario.ca/fr/lois/loi/97f41#s7s3">
           (3)
          </a>
          Subsection (1)
          <strong>
           does not apply to a person who destroys, takes or possesses the nest or eggs of a bird described in that subsection,
          </strong>
          <br/>
          (a)
          <strong>
           in accordance with the authorization of the Minister
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Ah yes, and that was the dilemma the MNRF faced. This appeared to concern at least Erin in her query to her co-worker. But that’s the last “concern” you will see from this Ministry.
          <br/>
          <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="300" scrolling="yes" src="https://drive.google.com/file/d/0B24A4SH_cewXLU1PcGRsb0VZblE/preview?usp=drivesdk" width="100%">
          </iframe>
         </p>
         <p>
          The public kept the pressure on, sending pictures and maps. Surely to God the MNRF would intervene and save the nest…?
          <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="300" scrolling="yes" src="https://drive.google.com/file/d/0B24A4SH_cewXdldSRmViZTVOTDA/preview?usp=drivesdk" width="100%">
          </iframe>
         </p>
         <p>
          That day, December 4th, the MNRF Manager asked Jim Beal and Joad Durst, “…how quickly we can we pull this (a response to the public) together”. They knew an eagle nest was protected under the Renewable Energy Act (REA) –
          <em>
           if
          </em>
          the nest was noticed during the Natural Heritage Assessment (NHA). But the company missed this nest in their NHA – was that as good as saying the nest “wasn’t there”? Should NextEra have to move their road and turbine plans now, they would have to go through the Ministry of Environment’s (MOE) amendment process all over again – and that would cost wind company time and money. NextEra wanted to
          <em>
           build now,
          </em>
          and they were going to get their way.
          <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="300" scrolling="yes" src="https://drive.google.com/file/d/0B24A4SH_cewXRlN4V0ZzcXJzTFU/preview?usp=drivesdk" width="100%">
          </iframe>
          <a class="more-link" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/03/nextera-freely-handed-permit-to-destroy-bald-eagle-nest-foi-records/#more-64980">
           Continue reading
           <span class="meta-nav">
            →
           </span>
          </a>
         </p>
         <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
          <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon sd-sharing">

       <article class="post-65113 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-ontario-government" id="post-65113">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/03/lower-electricity-rates-dont-fall-for-premier-wynnes-power-move/" rel="bookmark">
           Lower electricity rates? Don’t fall for Premier Wynne’s power move
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/03/lower-electricity-rates-dont-fall-for-premier-wynnes-power-move/" rel="bookmark" title="07:47">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-03-03T07:47:51+00:00">
            03/03/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/03/lower-electricity-rates-dont-fall-for-premier-wynnes-power-move/#comments">
           2
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p class="selectionShareable">
          <a href="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/wynne-neglect.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignright size-medium wp-image-55971" data-attachment-id="55971" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="WYNNE NEGLECT" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/wynne-neglect.jpg?fit=523%2C356" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/wynne-neglect.jpg?fit=300%2C204" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/wynne-neglect.jpg?fit=523%2C356" data-orig-size="523,356" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2013/05/30/todays-announcement-by-wynne-pure-spin-opa-permits-have-already-been-awarded/wynne-neglect/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="204" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/wynne-neglect.jpg?resize=300%2C204" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/wynne-neglect.jpg?resize=300%2C204 300w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/wynne-neglect.jpg?resize=150%2C102 150w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/wynne-neglect.jpg?w=523 523w" width="300"/>
          </a>
          <a href="http://www.theglobeandmail.com//opinion/editorials/lower-electricity-rates-dont-fall-for-premier-wynnes-power-move/article34195391/?cmpid=rss1&amp;click=sf_globe" target="_blank">
           The Globe and Mail
          </a>
          <br/>
          The rise in the cost of electricity in Ontario over the Liberal Party’s time in office has been staggering, and painful. Here’s just one example of how it has gone up:
         </p>
         <p class="selectionShareable">
          In November, 2007, the highest rate for households, during peak hours, was 8.7 cents per kilowatt/hour. Less than a decade later, it’s the
          <em>
           lowest
          </em>
          rate – the one you get for using your dryer at midnight. The highest rate, for use during peak hours, is 18 cents per kWh.
         </p>
         <p class="selectionShareable">
          That 107-per-cent increase in the peak rate is roughly six times the rate of inflation over the same period. The province’s manufacturing sector, meanwhile, has been walloped by the highest industrial rates in Canada, and among the highest in North America, according to the Association of Major Power Consumers in Ontario.
         </p>
         <p class="selectionShareable">
          The blame for this falls squarely on the consecutive Liberal governments of former premier Dalton McGuinty and his successor, Premier Kathleen Wynne, in power since 2003. Their mismanagement of Ontario’s power system has led to today.
          <a href="http://www.theglobeandmail.com//opinion/editorials/lower-electricity-rates-dont-fall-for-premier-wynnes-power-move/article34195391/?cmpid=rss1&amp;click=sf_globe" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>
         <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
          <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon sd-sharing">

       <article class="post-65111 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-bats-and-birds category-environmental-review-tribunal-ontario-government" id="post-65111">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/03/bats-stand-in-the-way-of-wind-turbines/" rel="bookmark">
           Bats stand in the way of wind turbines
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/03/bats-stand-in-the-way-of-wind-turbines/" rel="bookmark" title="07:22">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-03-03T07:22:37+00:00">
            03/03/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/03/03/bats-stand-in-the-way-of-wind-turbines/#respond">
           <span class="leave-reply">
            Reply
           </span>
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignright size-medium wp-image-62382" data-attachment-id="62382" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"5.6","credit":"","camera":"Canon EOS DIGITAL REBEL XT","caption":"UNDATED -  Erin Baerwalk examining a dead Hoary bat on Wild Energy Facilities near Pincher Creek, Alberta in August 2006.  Handout Photo: Monty Nicol    For Margaret Munro (Canwest) Story","created_timestamp":"1154320063","copyright":"","focal_length":"76","iso":"100","shutter_speed":"0.0025","title":"CNSPhoto-Munro-Bats","orientation":"1"}' data-image-title="CNSPhoto-Munro-Bats" data-large-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?fit=584%2C389" data-medium-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?fit=300%2C199" data-orig-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?fit=620%2C413" data-orig-size="620,413" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2014/11/19/wind-turbines-causing-thousands-of-bats-to-die-of-collapsed-lungs-annually-in-alberta-top-bat-expert/cnsphoto-munro-bats/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="199" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?resize=300%2C199" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?resize=300%2C199 300w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?resize=150%2C99 150w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/bat.jpg?w=620 620w" width="300"/>
          </a>
          <a href="http://www.theenterprisebulletin.com/2017/03/02/bats-stand-in-the-way-of-wind-turbines" target="_blank">
           The Enterprise Bulletin
          </a>
          <br/>
          COLLINGWOOD – Citizen scientists have proven beyond a doubt there is a population of endangered little brown bats in the area where wpd Canada Inc. plans to erect eight 500-foot wind turbines. Evidence from three bat biologists was presented at the Feb. 28 appeal hearing of the Environmental Review Tribunal chaired by Dirk Vander Bent with panel member Hugh Wilkins in the Collingwood council chamber Feb. 28.
         </p>
         <p>
          Witness and bat ecologist Sarah Mainguy said building turbines on the Clearview Township property would cause “serious and irreversible harm” to the endangered species. She was a witness for Preserve Clearview, a citizen group fighting the turbines. Mainguy provided the panel with a map showing the prevalence of habitat of the little brown bat (Myotis lucifugus) and other species in the wind turbine area in Clearview Township.
         </p>
         <p>
          She said citizen scientists Betty Schneider and Susan Richardson collected 2,000 bat call recordings obtained over 43 nights from different houses. “I went through the recordings to identify myotis. I screened all the calls and came up with the conclusion that 152 calls were identified as myotis and 146 were confident of myotis, all of which are endangered,” she said. Mainguy said the women were not allowed on Beattie family land where the turbines would be built but were allowed on other properties in the near vicinity.
         </p>
         <p>
          “We knew there were myotis but there are more than was earlier suggested. They are reasonably spread out in the area in red brick houses, which is their favourite.”
         </p>
         <p>
          wpd has not provided information on where the bats are located, she added. “We feel there is a large gap in the information provided in the pre-construction studies on where the bats are located. I feel this is a considerable gap especially in light of us finding quite a large number of bats,” she said.
          <a href="http://www.theenterprisebulletin.com/2017/03/02/bats-stand-in-the-way-of-wind-turbines" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>

       <article class="post-65081 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-canadian-government category-environmental category-viability" id="post-65081">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/21/defunct-wind-turbines-to-be-dismantled-on-sable-island/" rel="bookmark">
           Defunct Wind Turbines to be dismantled on Sable Island
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/21/defunct-wind-turbines-to-be-dismantled-on-sable-island/" rel="bookmark" title="18:48">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-02-21T18:48:38+00:00">
            02/21/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/21/defunct-wind-turbines-to-be-dismantled-on-sable-island/#comments">
           8
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignright size-medium wp-image-65082" data-attachment-id="65082" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="sable-island-wild-horses" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg?fit=584%2C329" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg?fit=300%2C169" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg?fit=620%2C349" data-orig-size="620,349" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/21/defunct-wind-turbines-to-be-dismantled-on-sable-island/sable-island-wild-horses/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="169" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg?resize=300%2C169" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg?resize=300%2C169 300w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg?resize=150%2C84 150w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg?resize=500%2C281 500w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/sable-island-wild-horses.jpg?w=620 620w" width="300"/>
          </a>
          Sable Island – such a ridiculous place to even think of putting wind turbines, but the Feds went ahead and did it.
          <a href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/nova-scotia/sable-island-wind-project-discontinued-1.3990349" target="_blank">
           Canadian Press
          </a>
          describes how the turbines never really did anything… they were dead from the get go.
         </p>
         <p>
          “The harsh conditions and extreme isolation of Sable Island have forced Ottawa to abandon a wind project on the iconic crescent-shaped sandbar — more than 15 years after it launched the initiative. Parks Canada said wind turbines don’t meet the needs of the wind-swept Nova Scotia island, famous for the wild horses that have roamed there since the 18th century.”
          <br/>
          —
          <br/>
          “When asked for the total cost of the project to date, Environment Canada said just under $1 million had been spent on the project as of 2006. It will cost another $150,000 to decommission the turbines, it said. The original budget for the wind project was $669,000.”
          <br/>
          —
          <br/>
          “Parks Canada said it hopes to develop “a reduced facility footprint, more efficient operations, reduced electricity demand, and renewable power generation” on Sable. The decommissioning will happen in two phases: The battery and switch gear were removed in 2015, and the towers and turbines are scheduled to be dismantled and removed this fall, Parks Canada said.”
         </p>
         <hr/>
         <p>
          It’s news that they are taking the turbines down, but it isn’t news that the damn things never worked. Here’s a
          <a href="http://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/nova-scotia/wind-power-on-sable-island-still-delayed-1.1076088" target="_blank">
           CBC story from 2011
          </a>
          . Remember – components started arriving at the island to be assembled way back in 2002. By 2011 they still weren’t producing power for the island!
         </p>
         <p>
          “Officials estimate it will cost another $660,000 to refurbish or replace what is now aging or obsolete equipment. It took years to assemble, secure and properly connect the five towers that now hold the wind turbines. In the summer of 2005, just after the turbines were hooked up and generating power, a piece of equipment called the inverter malfunctioned.”
         </p>
         <p>
          “Environment Canada said in an email to CBC News that “
          <em>
           during commissioning, it was discovered that a manufacturing defect —improper software — resulted in improper currents, and some transistors were damaged
          </em>
          .” Even though the damaged equipment was replaced and the proper software installed not long after the test, the system remains offline.
         </p>
         <p>
          “Although the wind turbines are generating electricity … other improvements are needed to create a system that effectively uses the electrical power generated by the turbines,” said Environment Canada spokesperson Mark Johnson. Environment Canada said it has completed an assessment of the entire system to determine whether any of it needs replacement.”
          <br/>
          ———
         </p>
         <p>
          It was broken. They tried to fix it and it still didn’t work. So they just let it all rot away, because – thank God! – they had diesel generators going the whole time!
         </p>
         <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
