       <article class="post-65078 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-noise" id="post-65078">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/17/wind-turbine-leaseholder-theyre-louder-than-i-expected/" rel="bookmark">
           Wind turbine leaseholder: “They’re louder than I expected”
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/17/wind-turbine-leaseholder-theyre-louder-than-i-expected/" rel="bookmark" title="07:41">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-02-17T07:41:16+00:00">
            02/17/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/17/wind-turbine-leaseholder-theyre-louder-than-i-expected/#comments">
           43
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/port-ryerse.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignright size-medium wp-image-53178" data-attachment-id="53178" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="Port Ryerse" data-large-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/port-ryerse.jpg?fit=584%2C656" data-medium-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/port-ryerse.jpg?fit=267%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/port-ryerse.jpg?fit=705%2C792" data-orig-size="705,792" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2013/02/25/port-ryerse-wind-development-final-public-meeting-feb-26/port-ryerse/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="300" sizes="(max-width: 267px) 100vw, 267px" src="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/port-ryerse.jpg?resize=267%2C300" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/port-ryerse.jpg?resize=267%2C300 267w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/port-ryerse.jpg?resize=133%2C150 133w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/02/port-ryerse.jpg?w=705 705w" width="267"/>
          </a>
          By Monte Sonnenberg,
          <a href="http://www.simcoereformer.ca/2017/02/16/an-earful-over-turbine-noise" target="_blank">
           Simcoe Reformer
          </a>
          <br/>
          The company that brought a four-turbine wind farm to Port Ryerse last year got an earful about noise levels at a community meeting this week. Boralex officials were on the hot seat Wednesday as 40 people from the Port Ryerse area had at them in a committee room at the Simcoe Recreation Centre. The occasion was a bi-annual meeting Boralex has agreed to have with its neighbours. Also attending were members of the Port Ryerse Community Liaison Committee.
         </p>
         <p>
          “It’s very loud and it’s very upsetting,” Port Ryerse resident Shana Greatrex told the gathering. “Our whole village has been affected. This is something we warned about a long time ago and no one did anything about it.”
         </p>
         <p>
          Village residents were surprised when one of the property owners who agreed to host a turbine said his neighbours aren’t imagining things. “I’m surprised I can hear them as loud as I do, and I wear an earpiece,” said Wally Faulkner. “They’re louder than I expected.”
         </p>
         <p>
          Comments at this week’s meeting are consistent with complaints across the province that wind turbines are noisy, disruptive and interfere with the peaceful enjoyment of property. In telling her story, Gail Lyons started off calm enough. However, the bitterness she feels came through loud and clear in her words. Lyons told the gathering she lives across the road from “one of these pieces of crap that I hate” and that she is often awakened in the middle of the night because her bed is shaking.
          <a href="http://www.simcoereformer.ca/2017/02/16/an-earful-over-turbine-noise" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>

       <!-- #post-65078 -->
       <article class="post-65032 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-setbacks category-wind-industry" id="post-65032">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/06/whats-64-stories-tall-4-2mw-wind-turbines-planned-for-wallaceburg/" rel="bookmark">
           What’s 64 stories tall? 4.2MW wind turbines planned for Wallaceburg!!
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/06/whats-64-stories-tall-4-2mw-wind-turbines-planned-for-wallaceburg/" rel="bookmark" title="18:24">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-02-06T18:24:05+00:00">
            02/06/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/06/whats-64-stories-tall-4-2mw-wind-turbines-planned-for-wallaceburg/#comments">
           13
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg">
           <img class="alignright wp-image-49177 size-medium" data-attachment-id="49177" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="Towering Turbine" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?fit=584%2C438" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?fit=300%2C225" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?fit=1280%2C960" data-orig-size="1280,960" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2012/11/19/nah-this-little-windmill-wont-affect-your-property-value/towering-turbine/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="225" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" src="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?resize=300%2C225" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?resize=300%2C225 300w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?resize=150%2C112 150w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?resize=1024%2C768 1024w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?w=1280 1280w, https://i0.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2012/11/towering-turbine.jpeg?w=1168 1168w" width="300"/>
          </a>
          David Gough,
          <a href="http://www.chathamdailynews.ca/2017/02/05/proposed-wind-turbines-will-be-significantly-taller" target="_blank">
           Chatham Daily News
          </a>
          <br/>
          The 12 wind turbines that are proposed for the Otter Creek Wind Farm, will be significantly taller than wind turbines already erected in Chatham-Kent. The wind farm, which is scheduled to be built north of Wallaceburg, will have Enercon E-141 turbines.
         </p>
         <p>
          From the ground to the top of the wind blades, the proposed wind turbines at the Otter Creek Wind Farm will measure 195 metres (642 feet). By comparison, the world’s tallest wind turbine in Germany is just under 230 metres (754 feet). Initially 17-20 wind turbines were proposed for the wind farm project. It was scaled back to 12, which Otter Creek officials said was due to public concerns. Most wind turbines in Chatham-Kent are approximately 155 metres (510 feet) from ground to the top of a blade’s tip.
         </p>
         <p>
          “The reason why these turbines are a little bit higher and a little bit wider in diameter, is to effectively reduce the use of the number of turbines,” said Adam Rosso, who is Otter Creek Wind Farm’s director of development. Rosso said by using fewer turbines it will reduce the visual impact, as well as other impacts.
          <a href="http://www.chathamdailynews.ca/2017/02/05/proposed-wind-turbines-will-be-significantly-taller" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>

       <article class="post-65016 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-bats-and-birds category-environmental category-ministry-of-natural-resources category-wind-industry" id="post-65016">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/02/dear-nextera-destroy-the-eagle-nest-just-do-it-by-sunday-love-ministry-of-natural-resources/" rel="bookmark">
           Dear NextEra, Destroy the eagle nest, just do it by Sunday. ~ Love, Ministry of Natural Resources
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/02/dear-nextera-destroy-the-eagle-nest-just-do-it-by-sunday-love-ministry-of-natural-resources/" rel="bookmark" title="09:38">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-02-02T09:38:19+00:00">
            02/02/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/02/dear-nextera-destroy-the-eagle-nest-just-do-it-by-sunday-love-ministry-of-natural-resources/#comments">
           15
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/chopped.gif">
           <img alt="" class="alignright size-thumbnail wp-image-54902" data-attachment-id="54902" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="nest chopped" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/chopped.gif?fit=296%2C360" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/chopped.gif?fit=246%2C300" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/chopped.gif?fit=296%2C360" data-orig-size="296,360" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2013/04/15/nexteras-next-nest/chopped/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="150" sizes="(max-width: 123px) 100vw, 123px" src="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/chopped.gif?resize=123%2C150" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/chopped.gif?resize=123%2C150 123w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2013/04/chopped.gif?resize=246%2C300 246w" width="123"/>
          </a>
          I’m still going through the NextEra eagle nest destruction FOI documents and will post them all as soon as I can. But so far I’d say this e-mail from the MNR to NextEra, on New Years Day (when we know everyone is at work, right?), delivering the permit to destroy the nest, says it all.
         </p>
         <p>
          Oh, and how long do you think it took them to get this permit? Well, NextEra submitted a request on December 28th (Saturday afternoon…), and four days later they had it in their hot little hands. Now that’s service!!
         </p>
         <p>
          <img alt="" class="alignright size-full wp-image-65017" data-attachment-id="65017" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"1"}' data-image-title="Permit letter" data-large-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?fit=584%2C359" data-medium-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?fit=300%2C184" data-orig-file="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?fit=1013%2C622" data-orig-size="1013,622" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/02/dear-nextera-destroy-the-eagle-nest-just-do-it-by-sunday-love-ministry-of-natural-resources/permit-letter-2/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="359" sizes="(max-width: 584px) 100vw, 584px" src="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?resize=584%2C359" srcset="https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?w=1013 1013w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?resize=150%2C92 150w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?resize=300%2C184 300w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?resize=768%2C472 768w, https://i2.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/02/Permit-letter-1.jpg?resize=489%2C300 489w" width="584"/>
         </p>

       <!-- #post-65016 -->
       <article class="post-65009 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-environmental category-ethics category-ministry-of-the-environment-ontario" id="post-65009">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/02/application-to-rezone-amherst-island-park-a-necessary-step-to-keep-the-wind-turbine-project-going/" rel="bookmark">
           Application to rezone Amherst Island park “a necessary step” to keep the wind turbine project going
          </a>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          <span class="sep">
           Posted on
          </span>
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/02/application-to-rezone-amherst-island-park-a-necessary-step-to-keep-the-wind-turbine-project-going/" rel="bookmark" title="07:59">
           <time class="entry-date" datetime="2017-02-02T07:59:16+00:00">
            02/02/2017
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="by-author">
           <span class="sep">
            by
           </span>
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/author/windaction/" rel="author" title="View all posts by wind resist">
             wind resist
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <!-- .entry-meta -->
         <div class="comments-link">
          <a href="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2017/02/02/application-to-rezone-amherst-island-park-a-necessary-step-to-keep-the-wind-turbine-project-going/#comments">
           1
          </a>
         </div>
        </header>
        <!-- .entry-header -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/amherst-Island.jpg">
           <img alt="" class="alignright size-full wp-image-59821" data-attachment-id="59821" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":""}' data-image-title="amherst Island" data-large-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/amherst-Island.jpg?fit=584%2C371" data-medium-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/amherst-Island.jpg?fit=300%2C190" data-orig-file="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/amherst-Island.jpg?fit=650%2C413" data-orig-size="650,413" data-permalink="http://ontario-wind-resistance.org/2014/01/13/senator-says-wind-farm-approval-dereliction-of-duty/amherst-island/" data-recalc-dims="1" height="371" sizes="(max-width: 584px) 100vw, 584px" src="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/amherst-Island.jpg?resize=584%2C371" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/amherst-Island.jpg?w=650 650w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/amherst-Island.jpg?resize=150%2C95 150w, https://i1.wp.com/ontario-wind-resistance.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/amherst-Island.jpg?resize=300%2C190 300w" width="584"/>
          </a>
          Elliot Ferguson,
          <a href="http://www.thewhig.com/2017/02/01/wind-energy-project-needs-lakeside-park?utm_source=addThis&amp;utm_medium=addthis_button_email&amp;utm_campaign=Wind+energy+project+needs+lakeside+park+%7C+The+Kingston+Whig-Standard#.WJK1SmNKxf1.facebook" target="_blank">
           Kingston Whig-Standard
           <br/>
          </a>
          A popular lakeside park in Loyalist Township will need to be converted to industrial land for a wind energy project to go ahead, according to a rezoning application to the provincial government. Invista’s property along Bath Road is to be used by Algonquin Power subsidiary Windlectric Inc. as a marshalling yard for its Amherst Island wind energy project.
         </p>
         <p>
          The Invista property on the south side of Bath Road, however, is zoned for parkland, but the company applied to the Ministry of the Environment and Climate Change to have the Certificate of Property Use (CPU) changed to temporarily allow industrial use of the park. The public has until March 2 to provide comment.
         </p>
         <p>
          The land is to be used for the laying of underground cable to transmit electricity to a switch station and the use of an existing access road to transport materials to and from a temporary mainland dock. According to a notice published Tuesday on the Ontario government’s
          <a href="https://www.ebr.gov.on.ca/ERS-WEB-External/displaynoticecontent.do?noticeId=MTMxNjkz&amp;statusId=MTk5NzY3&amp;language=en" target="_blank">
           Environmental Registry website
          </a>
          , the rezoning is “a necessary step” to keep the wind energy project going.
         </p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>
           “Put another way, the project cannot proceed without the proposed amendment to the CPU,” the notice stated.
          </p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>
          “If they don’t have this, they can’t build the project? Now they are basing the whole project on the mainland dock?” asked Michele Le Lay, president of the Association to Protect Amherst Island (APAI), the group opposing the project. “It seems that they started too early, they don’t have a good plan, they don’t have good measures, they still are lacking permits,” Le Lay said. “Right now this land is used by people in Loyalist Township, to walk their dogs, it’s a park and there is a boat launch. We’ve been saying all along that they don’t have the permits.” Le Lay said she is concerned that excavation on the land may disturb contaminents in the soil left over from previous industrial use.
          <a href="http://www.thewhig.com/2017/02/01/wind-energy-project-needs-lakeside-park?utm_source=addThis&amp;utm_medium=addthis_button_email&amp;utm_campaign=Wind+energy+project+needs+lakeside+park+%7C+The+Kingston+Whig-Standard#.WJK1SmNKxf1.facebook" target="_blank">
           Read article
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.thewhig.com/2017/02/01/wind-energy-project-needs-lakeside-park?utm_source=addThis&amp;utm_medium=addthis_button_email&amp;utm_campaign=Wind+energy+project+needs+lakeside+park+%7C+The+Kingston+Whig-Standard#.WJK1SmNKxf1.facebook" target="_blank">
          </a>
         </p>
         <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
          <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon sd-sharing">
